I found that (1) Anseranas should be placed in a monotypic family; (2) Dendrocygna, Thalassornis, geese and swans, and Stictonetta are paraphyletic to the rest of the Anatidae; (3) Cereopsis is the sister group to Anser and Branta, and Coscoroba is the sister group to Cygnus and Olor; (4) Plectropterus is the sister group to the Tadorninae (shelducks) and the Anatinae (typical ducks); (5) the shelducks are monophyletic and include Sarkidiornis (provisionally), Malacorhynchus, Hymenolaimus, Merganetta, and Tachyeres; (6) the tribe \"Cairinini\" (\"perching ducks\") is an unnatural, polyphyletic assemblage and is rejected; (7) the dabbling ducks (including the smaller \"perching ducks\") comprise an unresolved, probably paraphyletic group; (8) tribal monophyly of the pochards (including Marmaronetta and Rhodonessa), sea ducks (including the eiders), and stiff-tailed ducks (including Heteronetta) is confirmed; and (9) the retention of Mergellus and resurrection of Nomonyx are recommended based on clarifications of intratribal relationships. Problematic groups, effects of homoplasy, phenetic comparisons, life-history correlates, biogeographic patterns, and fossil species are discussed, and a phylogenetic classification of Recent genera is proposed.</jats:p>", "DOI": "10.1093/auk/103.4.737", "type": "journal-article", "created": {"date-parts": [[2019, 10, 1]], "date-time": "2019-10-01T03:54:07Z", "timestamp": 1569902047000}, "page": "737-754", "source": "Crossref", "is-referenced-by-count": 9, "title": ["A Phylogenetic Analysis of Recent Anseriform Genera Using Morphological Characters"], "prefix": "10.1093", "volume": "103", "author": [{"given": "Bradley C.", "family": "Livezey", "sequence": "first", "affiliation": [{"name": "Museum of Natural History and Department of Systematics and Ecology, University of Kansas, Lawrence, Kansas 66045 USA"}]}], "member": "286", "container-title": ["The Auk"], "language": "en", "link": [{"URL": "http://academic.oup.com/auk/article-pdf/103/4/737/30081231/auk0737.pdf", "content-type": "unspecified", "content-version": "vor", "intended-application": "similarity-checking"}], "deposited": {"date-parts": [[2019, 10, 1]], "date-time": "2019-10-01T03:54:08Z", "timestamp": 1569902048000}, "score": 31.289627, "issued": {"date-parts": [[1986, 10, 1]]}, "references-count": 0, "journal-issue": {"published-print": {"date-parts": [[1986, 10, 1]]}, "issue": "4"}, "URL": "http://dx.doi.org/10.1093/auk/103.4.737", "ISSN": ["0004-8038", "1938-4254"], "issn-type": [{"value": "0004-8038", "type": "print"}, {"value": "1938-4254", "type": "electronic"}], "subject": ["Animal Science and Zoology", "Ecology, Evolution, Behavior and Systematics"]}], "items-per-page": 20, "query": {"start-index": 0, "search-terms": null}}}
